## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes Controller Runtime Reconciler Registration

## Your Task

Trace how a controller registers itself with the controller-runtime Manager in kubernetes/kubernetes. Find the Go source files that define the Reconciler interface, implement SetupWithManager, and wire the controller into the manager's reconcile loop.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

101-assistanttext-
The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

Kubernetes v1.32.0 **does not use `sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime`** internally. It uses its own controller-manager framework in `staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager`.

### 1. Reconciler Interface
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`** — defines `controller.Interface` (the base controller interface, requiring only `Name() string`), plus `Debuggable` and `HealthCheckable` optional interfaces.

### 2. SetupWithManager Equivalent: `InitFunc`
- **`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`** — defines:
  - `InitFunc` type: the per-controller "setup" function signature
  - `ControllerDescriptor`: pairs a name with an `InitFunc`
  - `NewControllerDescriptors()`: registers all controllers

### 3. Wiring into the Reconcile Loop
The chain flows through `controllermanager.go`:
1. `NewControllerDescriptors()` → collects all descriptors
2. `CreateControllerContext()` → creates shared informer factories + clients
3. `StartControllers()` → iterates descriptors and calls `StartController()` for each
4. `StartController()` → invokes the `InitFunc`, which creates the controller, wires informers, and calls `go controller.Run(ctx, workers)`

Controller-specific `InitFunc` implementations live in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/apps.go`, `core.go`, `batch.go`, `networking.go`, etc.

It requires only a `Name() string` method. Controllers may also optionally implement `Debuggable` (to expose debug HTTP handlers) and `HealthCheckable` (to report health status). The actual reconcile loop is not mandated by a common interface \u2014 each controller implements its own `Run(ctx, workers)` method internally.\\n\\nA more generic reconciler pattern (with a `reconciler func(namespace, name string, newObj T) error` callback) exists in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/internal/generic/controller.go` for the admission policy subsystem.\\n\\n## SetupWithManager Equivalent: InitFunc and ControllerDescriptor\\n\\nIn place of controller-runtime's `SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager)`, Kubernetes uses the `InitFunc` type defined in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`:\\n\\n  type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\\n\\nEach controller is wrapped in a `ControllerDescriptor` struct (same file) that pairs the controller name with its `InitFunc`. The init function creates the controller, wires it to informers from `ControllerContext.InformerFactory`, and launches the reconcile loop via `go controller.Run(ctx, workers)`.\\n\\nExample (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/apps.go):\\n  func newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {\\n      return &ControllerDescriptor{\\n          name:     names.DaemonSetController,\\n          initFunc: startDaemonSetController,\\n      }\\n  }\\n\\n## Wiring into the Manager Reconcile Loop\\n\\n1. `NewControllerDescriptors()` in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go` \u2014 registers all known controllers by calling each `newXxxControllerDescriptor()` factory (defined across apps.go, core.go, batch.go, networking.go, certificates.go, rbac.go, bootstrap.go, policy.go, storageversionmigrator.go, validatingadmissionpolicystatus.go, etc.).\\n2. `CreateControllerContext()` \u2014 builds the shared `ControllerContext` containing the SharedInformerFactory, REST mapper, and client builder.\\n3. `StartControllers()` \u2014 iterates all enabled `ControllerDescriptor`s and calls `StartController()` for each.\\n4. `StartController()` \u2014 invokes `controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()(ctx, controllerCtx, name)`, which wires the controller to informers and starts its reconcile goroutine.\\n5. After controllers start, `controllerContext.InformerFactory.Start(stopCh)` and `controllerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory.Start(stopCh)` begin the shared informers.\\n\\nThe per-controller reconcile loop (`Run` method) processes events from a `workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface`, calling an internal sync handler that performs reconciliation \u2014 the functional equivalent of controller-runtime's `Reconcile(ctx, req)` method.\\n\\nThe top-level entry point is `Run()` in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`, which calls `CreateControllerContext` and `StartControllers`, completing the wiring of all controllers into the manager's reconcile loop.\"\n}\n",
